<script>
	// Only load homepage hero video if the user is on a large screen
	(function($){
		var $window = $(window);

		<!-- Functionality to hide the 3 buttons on first section-->
					<script>
				jQuery(document).ready(function($){
					$(document).bind('scroll',function(){
						var toTop = $(window).scrollTop();
						var winh = $( window ).height();
						var menu = $('#banner-home').length >0 ? $('#banner-home').offset().top+$('#banner-home').height() : 300;
						if((menu-70)<toTop){
							$('.fixed-cta').addClass('showgroupbtn');
						}else{
							$('.fixed-cta').removeClass('showgroupbtn');
						}
					});
				});
			</script>
